 bhartiya samay ke anusaar yah 02 july raat 10

 The total duration of this eclipse is about 04 hours 55 minutes

 When the sun stops appearing in full, it is called by the name of complete solar eclipse
 is suryagrahan kii visheshtaayen kya hai ?- yah grahan purna suryagrahan he
 - This eclipse will be visible mostly in Chile, Argentina, Pacific and South America, and Brazil
 - bharat or padosi deshon main iske darshan nahin honge
 - Since it will not be seen, the rules of sutak etc
 will not apply to it
 - surya ke vishesh rup se prabhavit hone kii vajah se iskaa asar har raashi par hoga
 - The effect of solar eclipse will remain on every sign for about 15 days
 agar grahan ke nakaaratmak asar se bachanaa chaahate hai to karen ye upaay-- grahan ke din surya mantra kaa adhik se adhik jap karen
